class Animal:
    def speak(self):
        print("ุตุฏุง...")

class Dog(Animal):
    def speak(self):
        print("ุณฺฏ: ูุงูพ ูุงูพ")

class Cat(Animal):
    def speak(self):
        print("ฺฏุฑุจู: ูู")

def make_sound(animal):
    animal.speak()

    return x + y
